          <h2 class="entry-title">
           <a href="/blog/2018/june/20/west-herr-wednesday-terri-giczkowski.htm" rel="bookmark">
            West Herr Wednesday: Terri Giczkowski
           </a>
          </h2>
         </header>
         <div class="entry-summary">
          <div style="text-align: center;">
           <img alt="495 × 281" height="281px" src="https://pictures.dealer.com/w/westherrautogroup/0987/f2348779a0299c5d60c7129740408ecex.jpg" width="495px"/>
          </div>
          <p class="xmsonormal">
           <br/>
           <span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black'>
            As the Office Manager in the Title &amp; Billing Office at West Herr Honda, Terri Giczkowski works with almost everyone at some point throughout the day.
           </span>
          </p>
          <p class="xmsonormal">
           <span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black'>
            We took a trip to Lockport to get to know more about her, for this week’s West Herr Wednesday.
           </span>
          </p>
         </div>
         <a class="btn btn-default btn-sm view-link pull-right " href="/blog/2018/june/20/west-herr-wednesday-terri-giczkowski.htm" rel="nofollow">
          read more
         </a>
        </article>
        <article class="clearfix hentry mod">
         <header>
          <h2 class="entry-title">
           <a href="/blog/2018/june/13/west-herr-wednesday-dan-payne.htm" rel="bookmark">
            West Herr Wednesday: Dan Payne
           </a>
          </h2>
         </header>
         <div class="entry-summary">
          <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center;">
           <img alt="500 × 375" height="375px" src="https://pictures.dealer.com/w/westherrautogroup/0975/dc44b0a4724959ca6e2f6a49e175da9ex.jpg" width="500px"/>
          </p>
          <p class="MsoNormal">
           <br/>
           Several years ago Dan Payne was sitting at a fundraiser at Canisius College at a table his father in law’s company had purchased. After watching Scott Bieler’s speech at the event, his wife turned to him and said “you want to work for that company, don’t you?” Dan’s response? “I sure do.”
           <o:p>
           </o:p>
          </p>
          <p class="MsoNormal">
           We interviewed Dan, brand new Sales Manager at Chevy Orchard Park and this week’s West Herr Wednesday, to learn about how he got to where he is today.
          </p>
          <p class="MsoNormal">
           <o:p>
           </o:p>
          </p>
         </div>
         <a class="btn btn-default btn-sm view-link pull-right " href="/blog/2018/june/13/west-herr-wednesday-dan-payne.htm" rel="nofollow">
          read more
         </a>
        </article>

        <h3 class="h1 ddc-heading-1 widget-heading">
         Welcome to West Herr Auto Group
        </h3>
        <div class="truncate content" data-ellipsis=" " data-less-text-label="click to hide" data-more-text-label="read more" data-truncate-words="228">
         <p>
          <font size="3">
           West Herr new &amp; used car 
dealerships have been serving Western New York (WNY) and the Buffalo - 
Rochester area for over 60 years.  We are proud to be New York 
State's largest automotive group.  From our humble beginnings 
on Clark St. in Hamburg, NY in 1950 we have grown to
           <a href="/locations/index.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="18 locations">
            23 locations
           </a>
           , 21 franchises, and over 
1900 employees!  In 2015, we sold over 46,500 vehicles and 
serviced more than 320,000!  We are grateful to our loyal 
customers, and our dedicated and hardworking employees...
           <a href="/dealership/about.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="(read more about us)">
            (read more about 
us)
           </a>
          </font>
         </p>
         <p>
          <font size="3">
           <br/>
          </font>
         </p>

         <h1>
          <font size="3">
           Massive Selection of Used Cars for Sale in 
Buffalo, Rochester, Williamsville, &amp; Orchard Park, New 
York
           <br/>
          </font>
         </h1>
         <p>
          <font size="3">
           At
West Herr, you can choose from WNY's largest selection of pre-owned vehicles, each 
backed by a West Herr Guarantee. Our three types of used vehicles are 
Peace of Mind Vehicles,
           <a href="/value-cars-used-inventory/index.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="Value Cars">
            Value Cars
           </a>
           , and
           <a href="/certified-inventory/index.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="Certified Vehicles">
            Certified Vehicles
           </a>
           . If 
you are not 100% satisfied with your vehicle, you can exchange it within
30 days, no questions asked! Looking for a deal? Check out our
           <a href="/last-chance-used-inventory/index.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="Last Chance 
vehicles">
            Last Chance 
vehicles
           </a>
           - priced to sell! We have the car for sale in Buffalo
that you have been searching for.

         <h1>
          <font size="3">
           Auto Service, Car Repair and Auto Parts in greater
Buffalo &amp; 
Rochester
           <br/>
          </font>
         </h1>
         <p>
          <font size="3">
           Keep
your vehicle running at its best by visiting any of our
           <a href="/schedule-service-appointment.htm">
            service and repair 
locations
           </a>
           in or around the Buffalo - Rochester area. The 
factory trained technicians at our car dealerships in Buffalo, NY and 
beyond have been trusted by many in Western New York for their ability 
to quickly and accurately address everything from routine service issues
to complex repairs and diagnostics. West Herr even offers four
           <a href="/bodyshop/index.htm">
            Collision Centers
           </a>
           , located in
           <a href="//bit.ly/24kZkni" internallink="false" target="_blank" title="Hamburg">
            Hamburg
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="/custom/new-cars-orchard-park.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="Orchard Park">
            Orchard Park
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="/custom/new-cars-williamsville-inventory-listing.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="Williamsville">
            Williamsville
           </a>
           and
           <a href="https://www.westherrfordrochester.com/bodyshop/index.htm" internallink="false" target="_blank" title="Rochester">
            Rochester
           </a>
           , staffed with technicians capable of repairing all makes 
and models. If you prefer to do your own service and repairs, contact 
the professionals at our
           <a href="parts/index.htm">
            OEM auto parts 
center
           </a>
           to ensure you have everything you need to get the job 
done right.

           Car Financing
Help Available in the Buffalo - Rochester 
Area

the largest automotive group in the state has its advantages.

get approved and keep your rates as low as possible.  No 
matter your credit, West Herr can provide you with options - all in the 
no hassle, low pressure environment that has made the West Herr family 
of car dealerships famous. Visit us today to discuss car loan and lease 
options for you.

if(DDC.userProfile.vehicleAccessories && DDC.userProfile.vehicleAccessories[vehicleId] && DDC.userProfile.vehicleAccessories[vehicleId].accessoriesTotal != null && DDC.userProfile.vehicleAccessories[vehicleId].accessoriesTotal != undefined){
setTabSummary(tabName,true);
}
break;
case 'payment':
if(DDC.userProfile.paymentQuotes && DDC.userProfile.paymentQuotes[vehicleId]){
setTabSummary(tabName,true);
}
break;
case 'prequal':
if( (DDC.userProfile.preQualification && DDC.userProfile.preQualification.referenceNumber) || (DDC.userProfile.creditApplication && DDC.userProfile.creditApplication.referenceNumber) ){
setTabSummary(tabName,true);
}
break;
case 'finance':
if(DDC.userProfile.creditApplication && DDC.userProfile.creditApplication.referenceNumber){
setTabSummary(tabName,true);
}
break;
case 'reserve':
if(DDC.userProfile.vehicleReservations && DDC.userProfile.vehicleReservations[vehicleId]) {
setTabSummary(tabName,true);
}
break;
case 'protect':
if(DDC.userProfile.protectionPlan) {
setTabSummary(tabName,true);
}
break;
case 'lifestyle':
if(DDC.userProfile.progress && DDC.userProfile.progress.INLINE_DR_MENU){
setTabSummary(tabName,true);
}
break;
case 'pickup':
if(DDC.userProfile.progress && DDC.userProfile.progress.INLINE_DR_PICKUP){
setTabSummary(tabName,true);
}
break;
case 'testdrive':
if(DDC.userProfile.progress && DDC.userProfile.progress.INLINE_DR_TESTDRIVE){
setTabSummary(tabName,true);
}
break;
default:
break;
}
}
calculatePercentComplete = function(){
if(enablePercentIndicator) {
var totalTools = Object.keys(DDC.digitalRetailing.summary).length,
completedToolsGlobal = 0,
completedToolsVehicle = 0,
publishPercentUpdate = false;
for (var tool in DDC.digitalRetailing.summary) {
if(tool == 'payment' || tool == 'reserve' || tool == 'accessories') {
if(DDC.digitalRetailing.summary[tool].complete == true){
completedToolsGlobal++
}
if(DDC.digitalRetailing.summary[tool].vehicleComplete == true){
completedToolsVehicle++
}
} else if (DDC.digitalRetailing.summary[tool].complete == true) {
completedToolsGlobal++
completedToolsVehicle++
}
}
var percentGlobalComplete = completedToolsGlobal / totalTools,
percentVehicleComplete = completedToolsVehicle / totalTools;
if (DDC.digitalRetailing.percentGlobalComplete != percentGlobalComplete) {
DDC.digitalRetailing.percentGlobalComplete = percentGlobalComplete;
publishPercentUpdate = true;
}
if (DDC.digitalRetailing.percentVehicleComplete != percentVehicleComplete) {
DDC.digitalRetailing.percentVehicleComplete = percentVehicleComplete;
publishPercentUpdate = true;
}
if(publishPercentUpdate) {
jQuery.publish('dr-percentComplete-updated');
}
}
}
calculatePercentComplete();
jQuery.subscribe('userProfile-updated', function(){
calculatePercentComplete();
sessionStorage.setItem(summarySessionStorage, JSON.stringify(DDC.digitalRetailing));
jQuery.publish('digitalRetailing-updated');
});
sessionStorage.setItem(summarySessionStorage, JSON.stringify(DDC.digitalRetailing));
});
